# --- üîπ ‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á ZIP ---
def create_zip(file_dict, zip_name):
    with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_name, 'w') as zipf:
        for filename, content in file_dict.items():
            with open(filename, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                f.write(content)
            zipf.write(filename)
            os.remove(filename)  # ‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏î
    print(f"‚úÖ ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå {zip_name} ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß!")

# --- üîπ ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á ZIP ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∏‡∏î ---
create_zip(group_1_files, "melah1_identity_package.zip")
create_zip(group_2_files, "melah1_chat_memory_package.zip")

import os
import zipfile

def create_zip(file_dict, zip_name):
    with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_name, 'w') as zipf:
        for filename, content in file_dict.items():
            with open(filename, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                f.write(content)
            zipf.write(filename)
            os.remove(filename)
    print(f"‚úÖ Created: {zip_name}")
